				{
					document.getElementById("countdown").innerHTML = seconds;
					if(seconds == 0)
					{
						newbrowserclose();
						return;
					} else {
						seconds = seconds - 1;			
						setTimeout("countdown(" + seconds + ")",1500);
					}
				}
				function newbrowseropen()
				{
					
				}
				function newbrowserclose()
				{
					document.getElementById("countdown").innerHTML = "";
